[30;1m181 | [0m[35m    A random forest is a meta estimator that fits a number of decision tree[0m
[30;1m182 | [0m[35m    classifiers on various sub-samples of the dataset and uses averaging to[0m
[30;1m183 | [0m[35m    improve the predictive accuracy and control over-fitting.[0m

[30;1m185 | [0m[35m    This transformer extracts 3 features from each window: the mean, the[0m
[30;1m186 | [0m[35m    standard deviation and the slope. The total number of features is thus[0m
